# see Modding Resources/Internal Factions/ for more info on functions and code
setup_init_factions = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		set_country_flag = active_small_medium_business_owners
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_small_medium_business_owners = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates }
		set_country_flag = active_industrial_conglomerates
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_industrial_conglomerates = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_industrial_conglomerates
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = fossil_fuel_industry }
		set_country_flag = active_fossil_fuel_industry
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_fossil_fuel_industry = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_fossil_fuel_industry
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = defense_industry }
		set_country_flag = active_defense_industry
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_defense_industry = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_defense_industry
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = maritime_industry }
		set_country_flag = active_maritime_industry
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_maritime_industry = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_maritime_industry
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = international_bankers }
		set_country_flag = active_international_bankers
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_international_bankers = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_international_bankers
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = oligarchs }
		set_country_flag = active_oligarchs
		apply_oligarchs_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_oligarchs = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_oligarchs
			apply_oligarchs_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = farmers }
		set_country_flag = active_farmers
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_farmers = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_farmers
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = landowners flagcheck_landowners = yes }
		set_country_flag = active_landowners
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_landowners = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_landowners
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = labour_unions }
		set_country_flag = active_labour_unions
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_labour_unions = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_labour_unions
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = communist_cadres }
		set_country_flag = active_communist_cadres
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_communist_cadres = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_communist_cadres
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = The_Clergy }
		set_country_flag = active_The_Clergy
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_The_Clergy = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_The_Clergy
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = The_Ulema }
		set_country_flag = active_The_Ulema
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_The_Ulema = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_The_Ulema
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = wahabi_ulema }
		set_country_flag = active_wahabi_ulema
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_wahabi_ulema = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_wahabi_ulema
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = the_priesthood }
		set_country_flag = active_the_priesthood
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_the_priesthood = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_the_priesthood
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = the_military }
			set_country_flag = active_the_military
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_the_military = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_the_military
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = intelligence_community }
		set_country_flag = active_intelligence_community
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_intelligence_community = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_intelligence_community
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = saudi_royal_family }
		set_country_flag = active_saudi_royal_family
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_saudi_royal_family = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_saudi_royal_family
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = foreign_jihadis }
		set_country_flag = active_foreign_jihadis
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_foreign_jihadis = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_foreign_jihadis
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = iranian_quds_force }
		set_country_flag = active_iranian_quds_force
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_iranian_quds_force = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_iranian_quds_force
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = wall_street }
		set_country_flag = active_wall_street
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_wall_street = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_wall_street
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = chaebols }
		set_country_flag = active_chaebols
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_chaebols = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_chaebols
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = isi_pakistan }
		set_country_flag = active_isi_pakistan
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_isi_pakistan = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_isi_pakistan
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = vevak }
		set_country_flag = active_VEVAK
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_VEVAK = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_VEVAK
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = irgc }
		set_country_flag = active_IRGC
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_IRGC = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_IRGC
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = the_bazaar }
		set_country_flag = active_the_bazaar
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_the_bazaar = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_the_bazaar
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = the_donju }
		set_country_flag = active_the_donju
		if = {
			limit = { flagcheck_the_donju = yes }
			set_country_flag = indifferent_the_donju
		}
	}
	intialize_internal_faction_dynamic_modifiers = yes
}

##Internal Factions Debugging Tools##
set_to_max_internal_faction_opinions = { ##Primarily used for cheating :shrug:
	custom_effect_tooltip = set_full_internal_faction_opinions
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = irgc }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_IRGC
		clr_country_flag = negative_IRGC
		clr_country_flag = positive_IRGC
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_IRGC
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_IRGC
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = foreign_jihadis }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_foreign_jihadis
		clr_country_flag = negative_foreign_jihadis
		clr_country_flag = positive_foreign_jihadis
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_foreign_jihadis
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_foreign_jihadis
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = iranian_quds_force }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_iranian_quds_force
		clr_country_flag = negative_iranian_quds_force
		clr_country_flag = positive_iranian_quds_force
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_iranian_quds_force
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_iranian_quds_force
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = saudi_royal_family }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_saudi_royal_family
		clr_country_flag = negative_saudi_royal_family
		clr_country_flag = positive_saudi_royal_family

	if = {

		clr_country_flag = positive_wahabi_ulema
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_wahabi_ulema
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_wahabi_ulema
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = the_priesthood  }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_the_priesthood
		clr_country_flag = negative_the_priesthood
		clr_country_flag = positive_the_priesthood
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_the_priesthood
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_the_priesthood
	}
	if = {

	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = The_Clergy  }

		clr_country_flag = negative_The_Clergy
		clr_country_flag = positive_The_Clergy
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_The_Clergy
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_The_Clergy
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = communist_cadres  }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_communist_cadres
		clr_country_flag = negative_communist_cadres
		clr_country_flag = positive_communist_cadres
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_communist_cadres
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_communist_cadres
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = farmers  }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_farmers
		clr_country_flag = negative_farmers
		clr_country_flag = positive_farmers
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_farmers
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_farmers
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = landowners  }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_landowners
		clr_country_flag = negative_landowners
		clr_country_flag = positive_landowners
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_landowners
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_landowners
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = labour_unions  }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_labour_unions

		clr_country_flag = positive_labour_unions

	if = {

reset_all_internal_faction_opinions = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = reset_internal_faction_opinion
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_small_medium_business_owners = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_IRGC = yes }

	if = {

	}

		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_industrial_conglomerates
		set_country_flag = indifferent_industrial_conglomerates
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_fossil_fuel_industry = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_fossil_fuel_industry
		clr_country_flag = negative_fossil_fuel_industry
		clr_country_flag = positive_fossil_fuel_industry
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_fossil_fuel_industry
		set_country_flag = indifferent_fossil_fuel_industry
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_wall_street = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_wall_street
		clr_country_flag = negative_wall_street
		clr_country_flag = positive_wall_street
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_wall_street
		set_country_flag = indifferent_wall_street
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_international_bankers = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_international_bankers
		clr_country_flag = negative_international_bankers
		clr_country_flag = positive_international_bankers
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_international_bankers
		set_country_flag = indifferent_international_bankers
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_the_donju = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_the_donju
		clr_country_flag = negative_the_donju
		clr_country_flag = positive_the_donju
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_the_donju
		set_country_flag = indifferent_the_donju
	}
	if = {
		limit = { non_indifferent_the_bazaar = yes }
		clr_country_flag = hostile_the_bazaar
		clr_country_flag = negative_the_bazaar
		clr_country_flag = positive_the_bazaar
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_the_bazaar
		set_country_flag = indifferent_the_bazaar
	}
}

display_election_status_small_medium_business_owners = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = small_medium_business_owners
			has_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_election_hostile_smbo_status_tt
		modify_country_flag = { flag = campaign_funding_count value = -2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = small_medium_business_owners
			has_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_election_negative_smbo_status_tt
		modify_country_flag = { flag = campaign_funding_count value = -1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = small_medium_business_owners
			has_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_election_indifferent_smbo_status_tt
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = small_medium_business_owners
			has_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_election_positive_smbo_status_tt
		modify_country_flag = { flag = campaign_funding_count value = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = small_medium_business_owners
			has_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_election_enthusiastic_smbo_status_tt
		modify_country_flag = { flag = campaign_funding_count value = 2 }
	}
}

#First 3000 lines or so are only to display. Use it as a tooltip in focus trees or event options. Don't use in immediate.
visually_display_opinion_rise_small_medium_business_owners = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_rise_opinion_smbo_hos_to_neg #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_rise_opinion_smbo_neg_to_indif #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_rise_opinion_smbo_indif_to_pos #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_rise_opinion_smbo_pos_to_enthu #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		display_add_pp_100 = yes
		newline = yes
	}
}

#Shows what the decrease will be and sets flags
visually_display_opinion_fall_small_medium_business_owners = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_fall_opinion_smbo_enthu_to_pos #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_fall_opinion_smbo_pos_to_indif #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_fall_opinion_smbo_indif_to_neg #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = display_fall_opinion_smbo_neg_to_hos #display
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		}
		display_subtract_pp_100 = yes
		newline = yes
	}
}

#Shows what the rise will be and sets flags
visually_display_opinion_rise_the_bazaar = {
	if = {
		limit = {

	if = { limit = { has_country_flag = enthusiastic_IRGC }
		Root_opinion_of_adj = yes enthusiastic = yes
	}
}

# Check for deposed faction
check_deposed_faction = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.1 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_small_medium_business_owners
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_the_bazaar
			NOT = { has_idea = the_bazaar }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.1 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_the_bazaar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_the_donju
			NOT = { has_idea = the_donju }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.1 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_the_donju
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_international_bankers
			NOT = { has_idea = international_bankers }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.2 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_international_bankers
		calculate_interest_rate = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_wall_street
			NOT = { has_idea = wall_street }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.2 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_wall_street
		calculate_interest_rate = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_fossil_fuel_industry
			NOT = { has_idea = fossil_fuel_industry }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.3 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_fossil_fuel_industry
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_industrial_conglomerates
			NOT = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.4 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_industrial_conglomerates
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_chaebols
			NOT = { has_idea = chaebols }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.4 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_chaebols
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_oligarchs
			NOT = { has_idea = oligarchs }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.5 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_oligarchs
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_maritime_industry
			NOT = { has_idea = maritime_industry }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.6 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_maritime_industry
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_defense_industry
			NOT = { has_idea = defense_industry }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.7 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_defense_industry
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_the_military
			NOT = { has_idea = the_military }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.8 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_the_military
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_intelligence_community
			NOT = { has_idea = intelligence_community }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.9 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_intelligence_community
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = active_isi_pakistan
			NOT = { has_idea = isi_pakistan }
		}
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { days = 1 id = int_fac_deposed.9 } } }
		clr_country_flag = active_isi_pakistan
	}

#Shows what the rise will be and sets flags
display_opinion_rise_small_medium_business_owners = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		increase_hostile = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = hostile_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		increase_negative = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		increase_indifferent = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		increase_positive = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	clr_country_flag = opinion_freze
}

#Shows what the decrease will be and sets flags
display_opinion_fall_small_medium_business_owners = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		decrease_enthusiastic = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		decrease_positive = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = positive_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
			NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
		}
		decrease_indifferent = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = negative_small_medium_business_owners
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {

#Shows what the decrease will be and sets flags
display_opinion_fall_chaebols = {
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = enthusiastic_chaebols
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		decrease_enthusiastic = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = enthusiastic_chaebols
		set_country_flag = positive_chaebols
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = positive_chaebols
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		decrease_positive = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = positive_chaebols
		set_country_flag = indifferent_chaebols
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = indifferent_chaebols
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		decrease_indifferent = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_chaebols
		set_country_flag = negative_chaebols
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = negative_chaebols
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		decrease_negative = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = negative_chaebols
		set_country_flag = hostile_chaebols
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = hostile_chaebols
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		add_political_power = -100
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	clr_country_flag = opinion_freze
}



#Shows what the rise will be and sets flags
display_opinion_rise_oligarchs = {
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = hostile_oligarchs
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		increase_hostile = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = hostile_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = negative_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = negative_oligarchs
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		increase_negative = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = negative_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = indifferent_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = indifferent_oligarchs
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		increase_indifferent = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = indifferent_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = positive_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = positive_oligarchs
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		increase_positive = yes #display
		clr_country_flag = positive_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = enthusiastic_oligarchs
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
				has_country_flag = enthusiastic_oligarchs
				NOT = { has_country_flag = opinion_freze }
				}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = opinion_freze #exit
	}
	clr_country_flag = opinion_freze
}

##Dynamic Modifier System for Internal Factions. The dynamic effects are sourced here using dynamic modifiers and basic variables.
######Apply Modifiers#####
##Do NOT add to these variables. They will break and the effects will reverse whatever you add.###
intialize_internal_faction_dynamic_modifiers = {
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: initialization of dynamic modifiers for Internal Faction System"
	#Economic Internal Factions
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = small_medium_business_owners_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_small_medium_business_owner_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = international_bankers }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = international_bankers_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_international_bankers_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = fossil_fuel_industry }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = fossil_fuel_industry_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_fossil_fuel_industry_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = industrial_conglomerates_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_industrial_conglomerates_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = oligarchs }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = oligarchs_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_oligarchs_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = maritime_industry }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = maritime_industry_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_maritime_industry_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = defense_industry }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = defense_industry_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_defense_industry_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = the_military }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = the_military_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_the_military_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = intelligence_community }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = intelligence_community_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_intelligence_community_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = labour_unions }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = labour_unions_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_labour_unions_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = landowners }
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = landowners_dynamic_modifier
		}
		apply_landowners_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = yes

#IRGC/Iranian Quds Force
apply_irgc_iranian_quds_force_dynamic_effect_DYNMOD = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = hostile_iranian_quds_force
				has_country_flag = hostile_IRGC
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = IRGC_commmunist_drift_var
			value = -0.04
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = negative_iranian_quds_force
				has_country_flag = negative_IRGC
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = IRGC_commmunist_drift_var
			value = -0.02
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = indifferent_iranian_quds_force
				has_country_flag = indifferent_IRGC
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = IRGC_commmunist_drift_var
			value = 0.00
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = positive_iranian_quds_force
				has_country_flag = positive_IRGC
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = IRGC_commmunist_drift_var
			value = 0.02
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = enthusiastic_iranian_quds_force
				has_country_flag = enthusiastic_IRGC
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = IRGC_commmunist_drift_var
			value = 0.04
		}
	}
}

###New Scripted Effects to Quickly Reduce/Increase Internal Faction Opinion###
increase_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		visually_display_opinion_rise_small_medium_business_owners = yes
		set_country_flag = current_small_medium_business_owners
		increase_internal_faction_opinion = yes
	}
}

decrease_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = small_medium_business_owners }
		visually_display_opinion_fall_small_medium_business_owners = yes
		set_country_flag = current_small_medium_business_owners
		decrease_internal_faction_opinion = yes
	}
}

increase_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates }
		visually_display_opinion_rise_industrial_conglomerates = yes
		set_country_flag = current_industrial_conglomerates
		increase_internal_faction_opinion = yes
	}
}

decrease_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates }
		visually_display_opinion_fall_industrial_conglomerates = yes
		set_country_flag = current_industrial_conglomerates
		decrease_internal_faction_opinion = yes
	}
}
